

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Tahoe/BCSS_Marked_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Tahoe → BCSS Marked Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Tahoe/BCSS_Marked_Tahoe/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Tahoe → BCSS Marked Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Tahoe/BCSS_Marked_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Tahoe → BCSS Marked Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Tahoe/BCSS_Marked_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Tahoe → BCSS Marked Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Tahoe/BCSS_Marked_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Tahoe → BCSS Marked Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Tahoe/BCSS_Marked_Tahoe/Config/TDPatterns/Left.lua ---

--[[
    Left (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Tahoe → BCSS Marked Tahoe → Config → TDPatterns
    Parent: TDPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local R3 = tdModule(ELSModel.R3);
	local R4 = tdModule(ELSModel.R4);
	local R5 = tdModule(ELSModel.R5);
	local R6 = tdModule(ELSModel.R6);
	local R7 = tdModule(ELSModel.R7);
	local R8 = tdModule(ELSModel.R8)
	
	if enabled then
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R8:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			R8(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R7(1);
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R6(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R5(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R4(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R3(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			wait(0.2);
			R8(1);
			R7(1);
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R8:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		R8(1);
		R7(1);
		R6(1);
		R5(1);
		R4(1);
		R3(1);
	end
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Tahoe/BCSS_Marked_Tahoe/Config/TDPatterns/LeftRight.lua ---

--[[
    LeftRight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Tahoe → BCSS Marked Tahoe → Config → TDPatterns
    Parent: TDPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local R3 = tdModule(ELSModel.R3);
	local R4 = tdModule(ELSModel.R4);
	local R5 = tdModule(ELSModel.R5);
	local R6 = tdModule(ELSModel.R6);
	local R7 = tdModule(ELSModel.R7);
	local R8 = tdModule(ELSModel.R8)

	if enabled then
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R8:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			R8(1);
			R7(1);
			R6(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R5(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R8(1)
			R7(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R4(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R8(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R3(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			wait(0.3);
			R8(1);
			R7(1);
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R8:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		R8(1);
		R7(1);
		R6(1);
		R5(1);
		R4(1);
		R3(1);
	end
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Tahoe/BCSS_Slicktop_Tahoe/Config/ELSPatterns/Pattern1.lua ---

--[[
    Pattern1 (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Tahoe → BCSS Slicktop Tahoe → Config → ELSPatterns
    Parent: ELSPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	--Visor lights
	local T1 = elsModule(ELSModel.T1)
	local T2 = elsModule(ELSModel.T2)
	local T3 = elsModule(ELSModel.T3)
	local T4 = elsModule(ELSModel.T4)
	local T7 = elsModule(ELSModel.T7)
	local T8 = elsModule(ELSModel.T8)
	local T9 = elsModule(ELSModel.T9)
	local T10 = elsModule(ELSModel.T10)
	
	--Rear lightbar lights
	local R1 = elsModule(ELSModel.R1)
	local R2 = elsModule(ELSModel.R2)
	local R3 = elsModule(ELSModel.R3)
	local R4 = elsModule(ELSModel.R4)

	--Front pushbar lights
	local B1 = elsModule(ELSModel.B1)
	local B2 = elsModule(ELSModel.B2)
	local B3 = elsModule(ELSModel.B3)
	local B4 = elsModule(ELSModel.B4)
	
	--Front lower pushbar lights
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1)
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2)
	local F3 = elsModule(ELSModel.F3)
	local F4 = elsModule(ELSModel.F4)
	local F5 = elsModule(ELSModel.F5)
	local F6 = elsModule(ELSModel.F6)
	
	--Back lights lights
	local V1 = elsModule(ELSModel.V1)
	local V2 = elsModule(ELSModel.V2)

	if enabled then
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				B1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				B2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				B3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				B4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));					
				wait(0.12)						
					
				B1(1);
				B2(1);
				B3(1);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.08)					
					
				B1(0);
				B2(1);
				B3(0);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.12)					
					
				B1(1);
				B2(1);
				B3(1);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.08)							
					
				B1(1);
				B2(0);
				B3(1);
				B4(0);					
				wait(0.12)					
					
				B1(1);
				B2(1);
				B3(1);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.08)							
				
				B1(1);
				B2(0);
				B3(1);
				B4(0);					
				wait(0.12)					
					
				B1(1);
				B2(1);
				B3(1);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.08)
				end
			end)
		end)()
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				T1(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				T2(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				T3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				T4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
				T7(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				T8(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));						
				T9(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				T10(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));														
				wait(0.12)						
				end
			end)
		end)()		

		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
					F1(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F2(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F4(1, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));	
					F5(1, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					F6(1, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));					
					wait(0.15)						
				end
			end)
		end)()

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Tahoe/BCSS_Slicktop_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Tahoe → BCSS Slicktop Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Tahoe/BCSS_Slicktop_Tahoe/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Tahoe → BCSS Slicktop Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Tahoe/BCSS_Slicktop_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Tahoe → BCSS Slicktop Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Tahoe/BCSS_Slicktop_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Tahoe → BCSS Slicktop Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Tahoe/BCSS_Slicktop_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Tahoe → BCSS Slicktop Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;

	--front pushbar

	local H2 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.H2);

	local R2 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.R2);

			pcall(function()
			while true do
					R1(0);
					R2(0);
					R3(0);
					R4(0);					
					R5(1);
					R6(1);					
					R7(1);
					R8(1);
					wait(0.15)				
					
					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);					
					R5(1);
					R6(1);					
					R7(1);
					R8(1);
					wait(0.15)						
					
					R1(0);
					R2(0);
					R3(0);
					R4(0);

					R7(1);
					R8(1);
					wait(0.15)

					R2(1);

					R4(1);					
					R5(0);
					R6(0);					
					R7(0);
					R8(0);
					wait(0.15)

					R2(1);
					R3(1);

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Tahoe/BCSS_Unmarked_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Tahoe → BCSS Unmarked Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Tahoe/BCSS_Unmarked_Tahoe/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Tahoe → BCSS Unmarked Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Tahoe/BCSS_Unmarked_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Tahoe → BCSS Unmarked Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Tahoe/BCSS_Unmarked_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Tahoe → BCSS Unmarked Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Tahoe/BCSS_Unmarked_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Tahoe → BCSS Unmarked Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	--Front Lightbar lights
	local T1 = elsModule(ELSModel.T1)
	local T2 = elsModule(ELSModel.T2)
	local T3 = elsModule(ELSModel.T3)
	local T4 = elsModule(ELSModel.T4)
	local T5 = elsModule(ELSModel.T5)
	local T6 = elsModule(ELSModel.T6)
	local T7 = elsModule(ELSModel.T7)
	local T8 = elsModule(ELSModel.T8)
	local T9 = elsModule(ELSModel.T9)
	local T10 = elsModule(ELSModel.T10)
	
	--Front Lightbar lights
	local R1 = elsModule(ELSModel.R1)
	local R2 = elsModule(ELSModel.R2)
	local R3 = elsModule(ELSModel.R3)
	local R4 = elsModule(ELSModel.R4)
	local R5 = elsModule(ELSModel.R5)

	local R8 = elsModule(ELSModel.R8)
	local R9 = elsModule(ELSModel.R9)
	local R10 = elsModule(ELSModel.R10)	
	
	--Front lights

	local B2 = elsModule(ELSModel.B2)
	local B3 = elsModule(ELSModel.B3)
	local B4 = elsModule(ELSModel.B4)

	--Back lights lights

	local V2 = elsModule(ELSModel.V2)

	if enabled then
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				B1(0, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
				B2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				B3(0, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
				B4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));					
				wait(0.12)						
					
				B1(1);
				B2(1);
				B3(1);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.07)					
					
				B1(0);
				B2(1);
				B3(0);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.12)					
					
				B1(1);
				B2(1);
				B3(1);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.07)							
					
				B1(1);
				B2(0);
				B3(1);
				B4(0);					
				wait(0.12)					
					
				B1(1);
				B2(1);
				B3(1);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.07)							
				
				B1(1);
				B2(0);
				B3(1);
				B4(0);					
				wait(0.12)					
					
				B1(1);
				B2(1);
				B3(1);
				B4(1);					
				wait(0.07)
				end
			end)
		end)()
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do	
				T1(1);
				T2(1);
				T3(1);
				T4(1);
				T5(1);
				T6(1);
				T7(1);
				T8(1);
				T9(1);
				T10(1);			
				wait()					
				end
			end)
		end)()		
		
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				R1(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				R2(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				R3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				R4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Taurus/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;


return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;
	
	local indicatorValue = script.Parent.Parent.State.Indicators.Value
	local indicatorOn;
	
	if indicatorValue == -1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Left;
	elseif indicatorValue == 1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Right
	end

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then --If disabled and no headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
	elseif headlightsState then --If disabled and headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Taurus/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Taurus/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Taurus/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Taurus/Config/Modules/TdPart.lua ---

--[[
    TdPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		part.Transparency = (transparency)
		if colour then
			if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
				part.BrickColor = colour;
			elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
				part.Color = colour;
			end;
		end;
		if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
			local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
			a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
			if colour then
				a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
			end
		end;
	end;
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Taurus/Config/TDPatterns/Left.lua ---

--[[
    Left (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Taurus → Config → TDPatterns
    Parent: TDPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local R3 = tdModule(ELSModel.R3);
	local R4 = tdModule(ELSModel.R4);
	local R5 = tdModule(ELSModel.R5);
	local R6 = tdModule(ELSModel.R6);
	local R7 = tdModule(ELSModel.R7);
	local R8 = tdModule(ELSModel.R8)
	
	if enabled then
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R8:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			R8(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R7(1);
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R6(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R5(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R4(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			R3(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R3(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			wait(0.2);
			R8(1);
			R7(1);
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R8:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		R8(1);
		R7(1);
		R6(1);
		R5(1);
		R4(1);
		R3(1);
	end
end

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)

	--front pushbar 
	local F1 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.F1);
	local F2 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.F2);
	local F3 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.F3);
	local F4 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.F4);

	local H1 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.H1);
	local H2 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.H2);
	local V1 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.V1);
	local V2 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.V2);	

	--rear  lights

	local R2 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.R2);
	local R3 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.R3);
	local R4 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.R4);
	local R5 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.R5);
	local R6 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.R6);
	local R7 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.R7);
	local R8 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.R8);

	local T1 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.T1);
	local T2 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.T2);
	local T3 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.T3);
	local T4 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.T4);

	local T6 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.T6);

	local T9 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.T9);
	local T10 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.T10);


	if enabled then
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					R1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));					
					R5(1, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					R6(1, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));					
					R7(1, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					R8(1, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					wait(0.12)				

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);					
					R5(1);
					R6(1);					
					R7(1);
					R8(1);
					wait(0.02)						
					
					R1(0);
					R2(0);
					R3(0);
					R4(0);					
					R5(1);
					R6(1);					
					R7(1);
					R8(1);
					wait(0.12)				

					R1(1);

		V2(1);		
	end

					wait(0.02)						

					H1(0);
					H2(1);			
					wait(0.12)	

					H1(1);
					H2(1);			
					wait(0.02)					

					H1(0);
					H2(1);			
					wait(0.12)	

					H1(1);
					H2(1);			
					wait(0.02)							
				end
			end)
		end)()			

		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					V1(0);
					V2(1);			
					wait(0.13)

					V1(1);
					V2(1);			
					wait(0.13)					

					V1(0);
					V2(1);			
					wait(0.13)

					V1(1);
					V2(1);			
					wait(0.13)					

					V1(1);
					V2(0);			
					wait(0.13)

					V1(1);
					V2(1);			
					wait(0.13)					

					V1(1);
					V2(0);			
					wait(0.13)

					V1(1);
					V2(1);			
					wait(0.13)		

				end
			end)
		end)()				

	else
		T1(1);
		T2(1);
		T3(1);
		T4(1);
		T5(1);
		T6(1);
		T7(1);
		T8(1);
		T9(1);
		T10(1);	
		R1(1);
		R2(1);
		R3(1);
		R4(1);					
		R5(1);
		R6(1);					
		R7(1);
		R8(1);
		F1(1);
		F2(1);
		F3(1);
		F4(1);	
		H1(1);
		H2(1);
		V1(1);
		V2(1);		
	end
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Unmarked_18_Charger/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Unmarked '18 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Unmarked_18_Charger/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Unmarked '18 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Unmarked '18 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Unmarked_18_Charger/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Unmarked '18 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/BCSS_Unmarked_18_Charger/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Sheriff Service → BCSS Unmarked '18 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Canada_Post/Canada_Post_Truck/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Canada Post → Canada Post Truck → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;


return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;
	
	local indicatorValue = script.Parent.Parent.State.Indicators.Value
	local indicatorOn;
	
	if indicatorValue == -1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Left;
	elseif indicatorValue == 1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Right
	end

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then --If disabled and no headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
	elseif headlightsState then --If disabled and headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Canada_Post/Canada_Post_Truck/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Canada Post → Canada Post Truck → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();
	local indicatorRear = body.Rearlights[(side == -1) and 'Left' or 'Right'];

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = neonMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = smoothMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
		indicatorRear.Material = indicatorRear.Parent.Centre.Material;
		indicatorRear.Color = indicatorRear.Parent.Centre.Color;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Canada_Post/Canada_Post_Truck/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Canada Post → Canada Post Truck → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;
	local reverseSound = body.Parent.Chassis.Platform.Sounds.Reverse

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			reverseSound:Play();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			reverseSound:Stop();
		end;
	end;
end;

	local T4 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.T4);

				T2(0);

				T4(1);
				wait(0.09)

				T1(1);
				T2(1);
				T3(1);
				T4(1);
				wait(0.02)					

				T1(1);
				T2(0);
				T3(0);
				T4(1);
				wait(0.09)

				T1(1);
				T2(1);
				T3(1);
				T4(1);
				wait(0.02)
			end
		end)
	else
		T1(1);
		T2(1);
		T3(1);
		T4(1);
	end
end

				B6(1)
				B7(1)
				B8(1)	
				wait(0.12)					

				B1(0)
				B2(0)
				B3(1)
				B4(1)
				B5(1)
				B6(1)
				B7(0)
				B8(0)	
				wait(0.16)

				B1(1)
				B2(1)
				B3(1)
				B4(1)
				B5(1)
				B6(1)
				B7(1)
				B8(1)	
				wait(0.12)	

				B1(1)
				B2(1)
				B3(0)
				B4(0)
				B5(0)
				B6(0)
				B7(1)
				B8(1)	
				wait(0.16)

				B1(1)
				B2(1)
				B3(1)
				B4(1)
				B5(1)
				B6(1)
				B7(1)
				B8(1)	
				wait(0.12)						

				B1(1)
				B2(1)
				B3(0)
				B4(0)
				B5(0)
				B6(0)
				B7(1)
				B8(1)	
				wait(0.16)

				B1(1)
				B2(1)
				B3(1)
				B4(1)
				B5(1)
				B6(1)
				B7(1)
				B8(1)	
				wait(0.12)							

			end
		end)	

	else
		B1(1)
		B2(1)
		B3(1)
		B4(1)
		B5(1)
		B6(1)
		B7(1)
		B8(1)	
		T1(1)
		T2(1)
		T3(1)
		T4(1)
	end
end


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Canadian_Armed_Forces/PA/CAF_PA_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Canadian Armed Forces → PA → CAF:PA Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Canadian_Armed_Forces/PA/CAF_PA_Sprinter/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Canadian Armed Forces → PA → CAF:PA Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Canadian_Armed_Forces/PA/CAF_PA_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Canadian Armed Forces → PA → CAF:PA Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights2;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		body.Headlights.Logo.Material = neonMaterial
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		body.Headlights.Logo.Material = smoothMaterial
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Canadian_Armed_Forces/PA/CAF_PA_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Canadian Armed Forces → PA → CAF:PA Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Canadian_Armed_Forces/PA/CAF_PA_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Canadian Armed Forces → PA → CAF:PA Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;
	local reverseSound = body.Parent.Chassis.Platform.Sounds.Reverse

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			reverseSound:Play();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			reverseSound:Stop();
		end;
	end;
end;

--[[

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Canadian_Armed_Forces/RWR_F-350/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Canadian Armed Forces → RWR F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;

--[[
    CarServer (Script)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Canadian Armed Forces → RWR G-Wagon

        RunContext: Enum.RunContext.Legacy

--[[local Knit = require(game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage').Knit);

require(Knit.Modules.Car).new(script.Parent, false);]]

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Canadian_Armed_Forces/RWR_G-Wagon/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Canadian Armed Forces → RWR G-Wagon → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;


return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	local indicatorValue = script.Parent.Parent.State.Indicators.Value
	local indicatorOn;

	if indicatorValue == -1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Left;
	elseif indicatorValue == 1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Right
	end

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then --If disabled and no headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
	elseif headlightsState then --If disabled and headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Canadian_Armed_Forces/RWR_G-Wagon/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Canadian Armed Forces → RWR G-Wagon → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	if enabled then
		for _,v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		end
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for _,v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		end
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Canadian_Armed_Forces/RWR_G-Wagon/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Canadian Armed Forces → RWR G-Wagon → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();
	local indicatorRear = body.Rearlights[(side == -1) and 'Left' or 'Right'];

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = neonMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = smoothMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
		indicatorRear.Material = indicatorRear.Parent.Centre.Material;
		indicatorRear.Color = indicatorRear.Parent.Centre.Color;
	end;
end;

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Canadian Armed Forces → RWR Supply Truck → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Canadian_Armed_Forces/RWR_Supply_Truck/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Canadian Armed Forces → RWR Supply Truck → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;
	local reverseSound = body.Parent.Chassis.Platform.Sounds.Reverse

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			reverseSound:Play();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			reverseSound:Stop();
		end;
	end;
end;

local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	--Front Lightbar lights
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1)
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2)
	local F3 = elsModule(ELSModel.F3)
	local F4 = elsModule(ELSModel.F4)
	local F5 = elsModule(ELSModel.F5)
	local F6 = elsModule(ELSModel.F6)
	local F7 = elsModule(ELSModel.F7)
	local L1 = elsModule(ELSModel.L1)
	local L2 = elsModule(ELSModel.L2)
	local L3 = elsModule(ELSModel.L3)
	local L4 = elsModule(ELSModel.L4)
	local L5 = elsModule(ELSModel.L5)
	local L6 = elsModule(ELSModel.L6)
	local L7 = elsModule(ELSModel.L7)
	
	--Rear Lightbar lights
	local R1 = elsModule(ELSModel.R1)
	local R2 = elsModule(ELSModel.R2)
	local R3 = elsModule(ELSModel.R3)
	local R4 = elsModule(ELSModel.R4)
	local R5 = elsModule(ELSModel.R5)
	local R6 = elsModule(ELSModel.R6)
	local R7 = elsModule(ELSModel.R7)
	local R8 = elsModule(ELSModel.R8)

	--Grill Lightbar lights
	local Q1 = elsModule(ELSModel.Q1)
	local Q2 = elsModule(ELSModel.Q2)
	local Q3 = elsModule(ELSModel.Q3)
	local Q4 = elsModule(ELSModel.Q4)		

	--Rear lights
	local P1 = elsModule(ELSModel.P1)
	local P2 = elsModule(ELSModel.P2)	
	
	if enabled then	
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				F1(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				F2(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				F3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				F4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
				F5(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				F6(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				F7(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));		
				L1(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				L2(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				L3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				L4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
				L5(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				L6(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				L7(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));		
				wait()						
				end
			end)
		end)()		
		
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				R1(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				R2(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
				R5(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				R6(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				R7(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				R8(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));																			
				wait(0.20)						
					
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);
				R5(1);
				R6(1);
				R7(1);
				R8(1);		
				wait(0.08)										
					
				R1(0);
				R2(0);
				R3(0);
				R4(0);
				R5(1);
				R6(1);
				R7(1);
				R8(1);		
				wait(0.20)						
						
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);
				R5(1);
				R6(1);
				R7(1);
				R8(1);		
				wait(0.08)	
					
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);
				R5(0);
				R6(0);
				R7(0);
				R8(0);		
				wait(0.20)						
							
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);
				R5(1);
				R6(1);
				R7(1);
				R8(1);		
				wait(0.08)	
									
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);
				R5(0);
				R6(0);
				R7(0);
				R8(0);		
				wait(0.20)						
							
				R1(1);
				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);
				R5(1);
				R6(1);
				R7(1);
				R8(1);		
				wait(0.08)	
				end
			end)
		end)()			
	
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				Q2(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				Q3(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
				P1(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				P2(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));						
				wait(0.25)						
	
				Q2(1);
				Q3(1);
				P1(1);
				P2(1);					
				wait(0.055)	
	
				Q2(0);
				Q3(1);
				P1(0);
				P2(1);					
				wait(0.25)	
					
				Q2(1);
				Q3(1);
				P1(1);
				P2(1);					
				wait(0.055)						
	
				Q2(1);
				Q3(0);
				P1(1);
				P2(0);					
				wait(0.25)	
					
				Q2(1);
				Q3(1);
				P1(1);
				P2(1);					
				wait(0.055)							
	
				Q2(1);
				Q3(0);
				P1(1);
				P2(0);					
				wait(0.25)	
					
				Q2(1);
				Q3(1);
				P1(1);
				P2(1);					
				wait(0.055)						
				end
			end)
		end)()					
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				Q1(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
				Q4(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));															
				wait(0.22)																			
					
				Q1(1);
				Q4(1);
				wait(0.045)		
					
				Q1(0);
				Q4(1);
				wait(0.22)						
					
				Q1(1);
				Q4(1);
				wait(0.045)						
					
				Q1(1);
				Q4(0);
				wait(0.22)						
					
				Q1(1);
				Q4(1);

				Q1(1);

				wait(0.22)						
					
				Q1(1);
				Q4(1);
				wait(0.045)						
				end
			end)

	else
		F1(1)
		F2(1)
		F3(1)
		F4(1)
		F5(1)
		F6(1)
		F7(1)

		L2(1)
		L3(1)
		L4(1)
		L5(1)
		L6(1)
		L7(1)
		R1(1)

		R3(1)

		R7(1)
		R8(1)
		Q1(1)
		Q2(1)
		Q3(1)
		Q4(1)	
		P1(1)
		P2(1)		
	end
end

local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	--Front Lightbar lights
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1)
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2)
	local F3 = elsModule(ELSModel.F3)
	local F4 = elsModule(ELSModel.F4)

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Canadian_Armed_Forces/RWR_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Canadian Armed Forces → RWR Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Canadian_Armed_Forces/RWR_Tahoe/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Canadian Armed Forces → RWR Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Canadian_Armed_Forces/RWR_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Canadian Armed Forces → RWR Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Canadian_Armed_Forces/RWR_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Canadian Armed Forces → RWR Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Canadian_Armed_Forces/RWR_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Canadian Armed Forces → RWR Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CFNIS/Intel/CAF_Caprice/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CFNIS → Intel → CAF Caprice → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.BrakeLights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v.Name ~= 'Top' then
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v.Name ~= 'Top' then
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end
		end;
	end;
end;

local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

	local T2 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.T2);
	local T3 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.T3);
	local T4 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.T4);
	local B1 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.B1);
	local B2 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.B2);
	local B3 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.B3);
	local B4 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.B4);
	local B5 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.B5);
	local B6 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.B6);
	local B7 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.B7);
	local B8 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.B8);	
	if enabled then
		T1(0);
		T2(0);
		T3(0);
		T4(0);
		B1(0)
		B2(0)
		B3(0)
		B4(0)
		B5(0)
		B6(0)
		B7(0)
		B8(0)
	else
		B1(1)
		B2(1)
		B3(1)
		B4(1)
		B5(1)
		B6(1)
		B7(1)
		B8(1)	
		T1(1);
		T2(1);
		T3(1);
		T4(1);
	end
end

--[[
    Pattern2 (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CFNIS → Intel → CAF Sprinter → Config → ELSPatterns
    Parent: ELSPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
local elsModule = script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart;

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local T1 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.T1);
	local T2 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.T2);
	local T3 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.T3);
	local T4 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.T4);
	if enabled then
		task.defer(pcall, function()
			while true do
				T1(0);
				T2(1);
				T3(1);
				T4(0);
				wait(0.09)

				T1(1);
				T2(1);
				T3(1);
				T4(1);
				wait(0.02)					

				T1(0);
				T2(1);
				T3(1);
				T4(0);
				wait(0.09)

				T1(1);
				T2(1);
				T3(1);
				T4(1);
				wait(0.02)					

				T1(1);
				T2(0);
				T3(0);
				T4(1);
				wait(0.09)

				T1(1);
				T2(1);
				T3(1);
				T4(1);
				wait(0.02)					

				T1(1);
				T2(0);
				T3(0);
				T4(1);
				wait(0.09)

				T1(1);
				T2(1);
				T3(1);
				T4(1);
				wait(0.02)
			end
		end)
	else
		T1(1);
		T2(1);
		T3(1);
		T4(1);
	end
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CFNIS/Intel/CAF_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CFNIS → Intel → CAF Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CFNIS/Intel/CAF_Sprinter/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CFNIS → Intel → CAF Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CFNIS/Intel/CAF_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CFNIS → Intel → CAF Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights2;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		body.Headlights.Logo.Material = neonMaterial
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		body.Headlights.Logo.Material = smoothMaterial
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CFNIS/Intel/CAF_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CFNIS → Intel → CAF Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CFNIS/Intel/CAF_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CFNIS → Intel → CAF Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;
	local reverseSound = body.Parent.Chassis.Platform.Sounds.Reverse

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			reverseSound:Play();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			reverseSound:Stop();
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CFNIS/Intel/CAF_Sprinter_BAe/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CFNIS → Intel → CAF Sprinter (BAe) → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CFNIS/Intel/CAF_Sprinter_BAe/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CFNIS → Intel → CAF Sprinter (BAe) → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:39
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end
